name:Gâ€uâ€eâ€sâ€tâ€ â€Uâ€sâ€eâ€r
info:Deluxe Double Room
info:Stayed in April 2024
info:Family
info:1 Review
rating:5
posted:Posted April 15, 2024
msg:The experience of staying here is very good. From the front desk to the restaurant waiters, swimming and fitness management, they are all friendly and kind, and will take the initiative to introduce and remind.
When we checked in, we were arranged on the 21st floor, a non-smoking floor. The whole room is spacious and bright. Looking out from the window is just a green space and a large lake. The scenery is very good. The details of the room are also good. There is a small trash can next to the washbasin and a trash can under the desk, which is very convenient. A super soft sofa chair in the room can relieve a day's fatigue.
The swimming pool is on the -1 floor. The entrance management will provide bath towels, and you can also rent a floating board (10 yuan each). The swimming pool has a safety guard and is divided into deep water and shallow water areas. The shallow water area is about 90 cm deep. The swimming pool is open for a long time, from morning to ten o'clock in the evening. The locker room is well heated, so there is no need to worry about catching a cold. We took the baby to swim twice after checking in, and the experience was very good.
The breakfast buffet is quite satisfactory, with everything you should have. For the buffet dinner, we ate a little because we swam late. The old duck soup and roast duck are good, with ice cream.
All in all, this is a hotel I will stay in again next time I come to Kunshan.
